<![CDATA[<p>once again. my parents have given unto me another life-altering theory, or more, concept that one would usually dismiss immediately but me.. </p> <p>i am now in an insomnial state because of that. ok so now i'm out late.. and my parents are fully aware of it. hell i use their gas half the time. i come home and it's all routine, as if it were 2 in the afternoon instead of 2 in the morning. it was all routine, that's what i figured. what i did <i>not</i> know, was that while i am out, my parents <u>still</u> worry about my whereabouts. sure they let me out, they argue not against that. just the fact that i came home tonight and my dad argued with me with deep eyes saying that being out so late into the night is dangerous.<br><br><b>fact</b>. quik cheks, 711s, and all the other quickie marts out there have been held up and televised more than too many times. <br><br><b>fact</b>. mall have been shot up if not inside, in the parking lots.<br><br><b>fact</b>. cars have crashed </p> <p><b>fact</b>. planes have collided <br><br><b>fact</b>. random muggings and shootings happen. <br><br><b>fact</b>. the odds of these things happening to me or anyone in this area of new jersey seems somewhat close to a million to none.<br><br><b>fact</b>. the fact that there is still a chance (columbine has been shot up. the twin towers have fallen. millions and billions have died due to war. ants have been squashed relentlessly for centuries.. .even milleniums) still presents the idea that you, being one out of 6billion+, could die at any instant. <br><br>damn you parents. <br><br>your worrying at first seems illogical but after thinking about it it's only true. although i, not to be self-focused, fully believe that i can fend for myself, i am not yet at... batman level... and can ward off 6 ninjas with shurikens mad fast in a matter of 3 minutes... but i'm not too worried for myself.. should i be? no. that's just being paranoid. that's what parents are for eh? <br><br>damn -_- it all makes sense now. after the comparing me to other kids, asking me why "it's not an A+, only an A", not buying me the shit i want. the leaving me to myself when it comes to those times when typical white yuppie parents would join in praise and acclamation: "gosh darn it, you're the greatest son ever - " no. it was those parents who spawned the children who became the adults of today who show no consideration for the future of their children. the "he smokes pot but hey, let's give him a car" family. the "he's failing spanish. oh and science. and math.. hey he's fai..... hey son, let's go to six flags!" no. has the world lost true value for the concept of hard work? metamorphisis through tough love, cultivation of independance on one's self and pure emotional and philisophical strength? <br><br>no, i'm not the hercules of mentalities, but more and more people are losing it to weakness. spoiled, smothered, saluted by parents today. these future parents will then spawn even more children - a generation of even more people - afraid to touch the snake because it's "gross", whereas people in the past a couple decades back weren't even moved by the sight of a spider on a table.... <br><br>is time un-jading society? <br><br>... no... it's just conforming society into a pristine world where there are no spots... no blotches of hard work and fearlessness. no need to look down at the dirt and grime because while our parents raise us to look up, we only expect the best, because we are the best and we deserve the best and the best of the best is us because we are the best <br><br>!!! no! <br><br>FACE THE WORLD! LOOK OUTSIDE AND TAKE IN EVERYTHING! <br><br>there are children out there who starve and work for a nickel a day, much more unpraised by parents for graduating high school because one: they have no high school, and most possibly two: because they have no parents! the people that the yuppie generation is slowly cultivating in the cul-de-sacs of america will in the future be the people who denounce the fact that there are people who starve, people who die due to lack of the simple ability to live. open your eyes, you fool, they're not there because they are lazy - they work just as hard as you do times two. they are there because fate laid them there, in a world without ups - <b>only downs</b> it is the parents who whip you into shape by psychologically torturing you - toughening your proverbial emotional skin into hide that can endure the wildest of barrages that life can throw towards your way. embrace the concept of tough love and hard work and independence that your parents may <s>throw at you</s> provide you with. there are very few people left who can truly explain the reason for bitter parents... but the purpose of these people is to balance out those people who do nothing to better the world - who enjoy the fruits of life only to spit the seeds out for some other guy to clean up... <br><br>embrace the development of yourself through tough love, because from it you become strong. roll with the punches, glide through the wind, leave your eyes open when you take the fall... because after you do, there won't be much in life that you can't go through without fearless determination and productive ambition... <br><br><br><br>yeh..... i'm gonna go eat my dinner.</p>]]> </content:encoded> <wp:post_date>2005-07-26 02:30:47</wp:post_date> aren't fenced off and hope to find something interesting...  i feel like fighting, i wanna ... ;realization;..  i may just be experiencing a Fight Club scenario...  ;shakes head;  anyway i dunno what it come from? one caveman just decided that "haha" expressions amusement?  no.  it's years of getting acustomed to it.  parents - teach - child, that's how it is..  </P> <P>it's like the matrix, everyone is absorbed in this life that is discreetly being controlled by a superior being.  except our being just so happens to be God..   in the matrix, they rebelled against the routine and system do you rebel??</P> <P>how can you step out of a circle which in this case is society, not to become an outcast, but to perform something so extraordinary that it sets bars higher..  people are always setting records, yeh sure.  "oh first man on mars", "fastest man on earth"... given we don't have super powers, there are always physical and mental records to be broken, ALWAYS.  so what else is there...  what other way is there to step outside the circle of normality?  </P> <P>my normal is waking up, working out, playing basketball, watching movies, working, eating, sleeping.  with the occasional communicating with other people.   this is my norm, this is my circle..   if i do something crazy like driving to nyc... that's not stepping out of the circle - i've done that already.  "go make music" - i've done that already..  "go meet a girl" - i've done that many times...  i guess i'm just ridden with bad luck like that but... done that already..  </P> <P>oh, it's not that i'm getting bored.  i love my life..  it's just that... this unknown potential is quite ...  oh i don't know.  intruiging.  every morning that i don't sleep my ambition backs up into my system and.... i burp.</P> <P>but seriously...  there's something to be done out there, that has not been done yet.  and it isn't expected by many.  and has only been anticipated by few...   and i want to know what it Mar 2008 17:54:13 -04:00</pubDate> -<content:encoded> <![CDATA[<P>my original intention was just to put up an old blog from two years ago.</P> <P>apparently, i screwed that good.</P> <P>i experienced some sort of enlightenment a couple days ago, i never had the incentive to do something about it.  now that i've stayed awake for a good 12 hours now, (having slept for all of yesterday) my bum ass felt bored...</P> <P>get this: people only trash other people because they're in someone else's territory.  think about it, it seems logical - some sort of <B>defense mechanism</B>.  people don't 'hate cuz they jealous yo', who the hell in their right mind does that. really. there's a deeper trigger than just jealousy that initiates on of the deadly sins.. <P>asians in america: "all those damn asians are smart as fuck"<BR>mexicans in america: "all those mexicans work like fuck"<BR>blacks in america: "all those blacks are tall as fuck"<BR>whites in america: "all those whites are white as fuck"</P> <P>don't be arrogant, don't just say "oh, you're just jealous".  screw off idiot, i've heard that before.  maybe that's not the case, you don't hate on someone for being in your territory because you're jealous of them.. "oh that bum, he should get a fuckin job" - <B>yeah, you're jealous because he's... broke?  </B>no.</P> <P><B><I>and when people do hate because they're jealous.  oh, you're just fuckin sad, boyo.  get your ass up and do something.</B></I></P> <P>you're not what you talk trash about, because it's not you, you're not familiar to it - it's foreign to your 'self'.  you see some short kid kick ass at basketball and something clicks in your head 'something is wrong'</P> <P>but let's say one day someone with a problem with mexicans goes to mexico.  he sees the life there and how things are.  he realizes, (well, chance in hell he realizes) that down to the grit and bone it's all the same - people work to get by they make a living by making a living.  so does he.  so does everyone else in this world...  he feels comfortble knowing this and suddenly, he may be on a lower plane than before or, they are re-elevated to what normal plane he should have seen them on before - his.</P> <P>everyone is the same (fight club).  everyone has a job or will have a job or did have a job that contributed to society.  those who don't are either unfortunate or just lazy rabbitasses.  but that leaves one to wonder, is there a 'occupation'... a fate that may hold not a regular joe job, but a task that involves something greater than keeping someone's checkbook, making cheeseburgers, or arresting crooks at night...  what else is there to do other than to wake up in the morning and go to bed at night...  what else is there to see other than the sun during the day... what else is there to think other than what is relevant to what goes on during the day...  </P> <P>humans have the potential to learn as toddlers, conceive babies as adults, pass on culture as elders.  everyone has this potential, but not everyone exercises it.  if this is true, there must be a higher potential that not everyone who learns, conceives, and passes culture exercises.  but what?  what is it that this higher potential can allow?  there is something more to life than stopping at red and going at green, it's the click in our heads that make us stop and go.  it's the spark that drives us to move - there is something behind it.  it is the one with that higher potential and drive who will figure out just what it is... and how to exercise it.  </P> <P>btw, the book The Giver...  being made into a movie.  ;heh..</P> <P>p.s.  (open your eyes, because the clouds are moving behind you.)</P>]]> </content:encoded> <wp:post_date>2005-07-12 05:21:57</wp:post_date> <wp:post_date_gmt>2005-07-12 09:21:57</wp:post_date_gmt> <![CDATA[<FONT color=#4b4b20><B>"if you want to be treated like a grown-up, then behave like a grown-up!" - my parents, oh.. two or three years ago..<BR><BR></B><B>monday:</B> middle school graduation.<BR><B>tuesday:</B> high school graduation.<BR><BR>what a coincidence. they were both at the high school. they both had the same presenters. they both had speeches. they both had graduation gowns. difference?<BR><BR>the middle school graduation emphasized the concepts they learned in middle school. the speech given at the high school graduation expressed how what was learned in high school prepared them for the life after. i've seen 8th graders condone each other because they will miss each other... and i've seen 12th graders congratulate each other because of what they went through, experienced - mutually. <B>don't cry because it's over, smile because it happened</B><BR><BR><B>the gift if growing up is knowing the world.</B> you can't give a puppy the scent of cocaine and expect it to sniff out the tijuana cartel. as you go through each day, you learn alot. or, you're provided with that opportunity at least... do you know the value of patience? do you know the value of fortitude? do you know the value of justice? do you know the value of wisdom? the four virtues; only through expericne can you truly <I>value a value</I>. <BR><BR><B>why upperclassmen seem to always hate freshmen.</B> when you're a freshman, you don't ask questions. you don't brag, you don't test, you don't act like you've been to the moon and back. because you haven't. the upperclassmen know this because they were there. "the freshmen-on-the-bus rule".. "we've all had to ride the bus". is it just that we weren't as privileged as the kiddies are nowadays? when freshmen give even the sophomores attitude, it is <I>never</I> taken lightly. by majority's standards at least.<BR><BR><B>"he's only worked here a week and he acts like he owns the joint!"</B> the same goes for real life. i guess that's how high school prepares you for real life; a microcosm filled with the same status-based rankings real life demands from society. <B>"we thought we left the war back home, when it was waiting for us right here" - Gangs of New York</B> it's like you can't change society. being flamboyant and cocky like you control the world - people look down on that because you can't control the world.. i guess that's another thing you learn in high school. the world works in routine. you can't change the demands from life, you can only change the way you give it what you've got.<BR><BR><B>"that kid gives me a lip, i'm cuttin his into two!"</B> bottom line? you ain't got <B>nuttin</B> until you realize you ain't got <B>nuttin</B>. and when you realize that, you'll find the same thing people found in you. if you've already found the previous, you'd most likely agree that this is how life works. it's like a clock, life doesn't care when you're born or dead. like a mega-corporation, there will always be more people to feed off of.<BR><BR><B>what's the point, if we all live and die and time goes on?</B>. again, man.. it's not what you do, it's how you do it. it's not who you impress, it's how you make the impression. you can impress the world, but the world will forget you. you can make a good impression on someone, and that person will remember you as a great person forever. you can make a bad impression on someone, and that person will remember you as a total idiot forever. it's your choice. give it some thought. for the sake of man-kind, <I>please</I>.<BR><BR>anyways.. on a lighter note, one time for the class of 2005.<BR><FONT will always be the same.  therefore you can change your fate, and from the day you were born, be destined to try to change your fate.  see, it works, perfectly.  <BR><BR>so you are set for something. Mar 2008 18:08:35 -04:00</pubDate> -<content:encoded> <![CDATA[<BR>why am i awake at 3 something in the morning? mixing shit like what's playing on this site right now of course, what kind of question was that. yeh.. i feel like a heart tumor has been scraped off to the size of a wart. why am i tired but not even sleepy at all. i'm fckin freezing. it's funny cuz all of that doesn't matter.. yehknow...<BR><BR><B>i almost died a few days ago...</B><BR>and it isn't until now that i realize how mother fcking grateful i am that those seconds away from death i was kept away from me.. k, i'm goin down this one street right, look left, look right like your typical road master... nothing coming except for a couple cars a long way down the road.. so i go.. out of fcking nowhere this brown car comes skidding down towards me on driver side... 'WTF' i'm thinking 'this bitch better stop'... but yeh it doesn't.. naturally.. i freeze like a deer in the headlights... i guess it was better i didn't try n speed away to avoid it or else the girl in the car coming right for me would'nt have stopped the way she did.. the car literally skipped down towards me cuz she slammed her brakes so fckin hard she had to have been going 40-50 or something like that, dumb hoe.. this was in the middle of a downtown raritan neighborhood, mind you, not the 287.. i'm fuckin lookin like a douche just sitting there with my shades on watching this car come towards me and it stops.. o damn does it stop.. license plate only a foot away from my door handle, i'm talkin, this girl is so close i can see the color of the pupils in her eyes. she just blinked. i think we both knew someone, most likely me, could've gotten at the very least seriously hurt - her car was aimed at my body almost perfectly. the intricate design of this.. escape from death was so impressively executed by fate that. i do believe as my friend did say that 'someone has GOT to be watching over you'.. i do believe it.. i dunno who or what or even why but i do. shit if that car had braked only a second later than it did, my ass would be in a wheelchair or sumin. i for one was scared shitless almost.. i drove the rest of the way to work after that with my right arm shaking and my neck tighter than a rubber band stretched 2 feet long... o holy shit was i scared.. i have never been that scared ever in my entire life.. i drove thinking to myself "dammit. just now, you could have died. just now. in that split second. the money you make tonight would not have matter because you could have died.." i don't care what physics say about the inertia or energy or whatever of the car and its relationship to my sorry ass in the middle of the street, i think i truly, almost died. i escaped certain injury, that's for sure - the car - and i swear - was somewhere near a foot - 12 inches - from my door. THAT is scary. fuck the ring 2 or mothman prophecies. hell, i will always remember the first time i almost got in an accident.. cuz it was the same day death came the closest to me...]]> happen and they pass me by with a simple hello.  and then out of nowhere things catch me at farewell.  i fuckin hate it.  it's like watching a wonderous colorful bird flying through the sky and saying to yourself, "hm.  that's a beautiful wonderous colorful bird flying through the sky".  only to find later on something like "o hey, that bird..  if you give the bird the finger it will lay eggs filled with love and dozens of hundred dollar bills in your sock drawer behind the polo sports".  and you say. damn.  if only i had given that bird the middle finger - i <STRONG>just might be happy</STRONG> and rich right now.  damn.  i hate that kinda shit.  cuz it just pisses the fuck out of me.  it just pisses me off.</P><FONT face="times new roman" size=3> <P><FONT face="times new roman" size=3>i hate how <STRONG>people are so complex.</STRONG>  the human brain can't even comprehend all at once how much the human brain can comprehend, all at once.  the human brain can cause you to feel pain, rejection, regret, annoyance, gloomy, horny, bias...  yada yada.  you're "<EM>supposed to</EM>" <U>not worry about what people think about you</U>.  you're "<EM>supposd to</EM>"<U> not think about what people will say about you</U>..  but hey, you're "<U>supposed to</U>" <STRONG>make sure you don't piss people off</STRONG>.  you're "<U>supposed to</U>" <STRONG>make people happy so you can be happy.  how do you satisfy the two concepts at the same time if they contradict each other</STRONG>.  tell me.  i hate how<STRONG><EM> people need to be nurtured so carefully or else the very fabric of society around you unravels into a chaotic medley of panic</EM></STRONG>..  i fuckin hate it.  i want to be somewhere where i can depend on people definitely without having to worry about what i do because it might affect other people, indirectly.  i fuckin hate the complexity of the human brain.  it pisses me off.  <STRONG>shut up</STRONG>.</P> <P><FONT face="times new roman" size=3>it really <EM>pisses me off how people blame other people for their misfortunes</EM>.  i'm fuckin pissed at the way i <U>miss out on my opportunities from years ago that i obviously haven't realized were opportunities until now</U>.  but hey, <STRONG>fuckety fuck fuck</STRONG>.  but there are still people who blame the inactivity of other people for the shitty lives they lead.  just because <EM>you aren't at the pinnacle of your society</EM> and no one lays layers of rose petals at your feet at your every whim doesn't mean it's anyone but your own fault.  hey, for all you know, someone has already mentioned to you the folly of your ways.  maybe you should have looked for warnings of things to come.  hey, for all you know, <STRONG><EM>someone MAY have already warned you before hand time and time ago</EM></STRONG>.  because of that, it's so, SO not anyone but your own fault you end up where you do.  don't play the baby shit.  cuz i bet even you're tired of it yourself - so just grow up.  stop trying so hard and live.  cuz <EM>it's pissing me the fuck off</EM>.</P><FONT face="times new roman" size=3> <P><FONT face="times new roman" size=3>i hate it.  <STRONG>what does happy feel like</STRONG>?  laughing because the snot popped out of your buddy's nose while he was drinking a soda on top of a freezer?  that's <U>just humor</U>.  thank god for it, yes.. but happiness?  happiness with god is <EM>nothing but contentment</EM>, please, even you can agree with that.  enthusiastically praising and all that, does it really make a human light up with natural joy? or does it just make so many content because of the fact that they're conforming to a culture that has continued for so long, over thousands and thousands of years.  that aside.  <STRONG>what does HAPPY feel like</STRONG>?  what does running through a monsoon rainstorm in the middle of lunch with nothing on but shorts and sandals feel like.  what does sitting in front of the tv screen with someone you can confide in, just wedgin there feel like?  <EM>happiness is all but human-made</EM>, but we are all human yet <STRONG>not all of us can generate this natural, yet so artificial feeling</STRONG>.  some of us aren't so lucky enough as to have that ability to create a true genuine smile at the snap of a finger.  <STRONG><U>it's easy to be content, yes, but what does happy feel like?</U></STRONG>  <STRONG>i don't know</STRONG>.  <EM>and that pisses me off.</EM></P> <P><FONT face="times new roman" size=3>wake me up when september ends.  i don't know what that part of the song means just yet, but i really don't care.  i don't care so much that <EM>i can't even help myself.</EM>  <STRONG>good bye.</STRONG></P></FONT></FONT></FONT></FONT></FONT></FONT></FONT></FONT></FONT>]]> <wp:comment_author_email>bounce@xanga.com</wp:comment_author_email> <wp:comment_author_url>http://xmegaaaan.xanga.com/</wp:comment_author_url> <wp:comment_user_id>0</wp:comment_user_id> <wp:comment_xanga_user_id>2181056</wp:comment_xanga_user_id> <wp:comment_parent>0</wp:comment_parent> <wp:comment_type/> <wp:comment_id>343091207</wp:comment_id> </wp:comment> </item> -<item> <title/> <dc:creator>illehchillehpnoi</dc:creator> <pubDate>Wed, 30 Nov 2005 18:06:32 -05:00</pubDate> -<content:encoded> <![CDATA[<CENTER><A href="http://www.petitiononline.com/BRHSNO/PETITION.HTML" target=_new>http://www.petitiononline.com/BRHSNO/PETITION.HTML</A><BR><BR><I>... heh ... heheh ...<BR><BR></I><BR><BR></CENTER><LEFT>First of all, if this was takin seriously by anyone - it would never have worked. second of all, i applaud the people who didn't take this seriously because it never will be? so kudos to you, internet geek, who spent a good 5 minutes or so thinking up a clever comment to degrade this attempt at making a difference. petitions are like movements against the mechanic democratic republic that gears our laws and standards. well... they're more like nudges, than movements. if you really want something done to change the school district schedule (which, mind you, is officially decided and declared official by the board before each and every school year - along with every single little detail that entails each school year; notice the "adopted/revised & adopted" footnotes at each of the district documents made public to all of us) you can't nudge giant entities like a school board. if you want change, you need to push with great force and precise execution. <BR><BR></LEFT> <CENTER><FONT color=#888888>The National Weather Service issued a wind chill advisory for areas including the state of New Jersey concerning Sunday evening and early Monday morning. "Strong Northwest winds ...10 to 15 miles an hour early monday morning ... Wind chill values will approach 10 below zero elsewhere [in New Jersey] tonight and early Monday" To assure that this is in more concern to a more broad spectrum of people than just the high school students, 10 degrees below zero is quite an extreme condition no matter who should be facing the 42 degrees below freezing temperature. Even with a 2 hour delay, workers will have to wake up early in the morning to prepare for a school day. Custodians will spend about an average of 120 minutes outside before the school session begins if not shoveling - salting walkways. Teachers and staff who live far from the Bridewater-Raritan School District will wake up as early as usual. But considering the ridiculous road conditions outside, they will still have to venture out onto what I would hope to assume icy roadways in order to reach our town (not to mention, especially our lovely California-style high school). Strong northwest winds 10-15mph... Even if snow is shoveled off of walkways, this storm brought a dry snowfall. That means the snow can be easily blown back onto walkways, parking lots, or any other area that may need access to during the day. Concerning the high school, it takes well around 13 minutes to get from the field house to the 800 building. Should the wind still show significant force by the time students arrive at the high school, many would be endangered to many possibly incidents where a student or faculty member may be vulnerable to illness or injury. Bundling up is indeed our own responsibilities but we cannot control the weather. It all comes down to one simple message. "We're walking in a foot of snow. The roads are impossible. ITS TOO DAMN COLD."<BR><BR></CENTER> <P><LEFT><FONT color=#000000>There, online petition. Stick <I>THAT</I> up your arse.<BR><BR>Bottom line to this blog is. People spend too much time bitching and complaining. Drama for yo mama and all that copacobana; JUST SHUT THE HELL UP! If you're not gonna take action against something you dislike... If you want something done, then take control of it. - <FONT size=2>Duh.</FONT> </FONT></P> <P><FONT color=#000000>No half-assing it here.</P> <CENTER></CENTER> <CENTER></CENTER></FONT></FONT>]]> 2008 18:07:07 -04:00 "<B>Your heart is free; Have the courage to follow it.</B>"<BR>;sigh of relief;. Christmas is almost... <I>Almost</I> here.. It seems like nowadays <U>everyone</U> has fallen in love, to a point where love, in all it's greatness and power... Has just lost it's touch.. To me, love is...<BR><B>Love is just that feeling of being home. That feeling you have when you're with people and you can just sigh, breathe... Because you have nothing to afflict you when you're with love. <BR>• Love protects you from all evils and ghosts and demons and vampires and booger monsters - the way parents comfort their children... <BR>• Love is the sudden outbursts of randomosity you feel comfortably natural with - the way you can be yourself around your best friends.. <BR>• Love is the way the snow falls down pure white, and lands on the ground, still pure white - that assured, comfortable feeling you get when you know you've done something knowing you can depend on the person you've done it for.<BR>•Love is that light at the end of a long winding stanky ass tunnel - the way people happen to find God after a long life of hardships<BR>• Love is like that feeling when you're just laying in front of a fire on a couch with that one someone, just laying there knowing you're home<BR></B>It feels like everyone has someone. Lucky them. This time last year, I was mad, irritated, impatient, jealous... Extremely jealous, and impatient... It was "Oh God, another depressing winter..." ;grin; I can't say i've totally gone 'monk-enlightened' now. But I've finally gotten to that point where I feel like my time here has been purged and I'm just set... Good to go cuz I know where I'm going with my life.. College, money, family, cars, so on and so on... Yeh, I can't say I'm satisfied now, cuz frankly I'm never satisfied with myself. But I can say this... Instead of wishing and hoping to be laying in front of a fireplace with that one someone, I think I'm just fine with maybe one more winter, driving around or talking walks by myself... Just admiring the view I've had for the past few winters<BR><BR> <CENTER><IMG height=263 src="http://www.zoomscope.com/tove/archives/image/februarhimmel1.jpg" width=300></FONT></CENTER><BR><B>Happy Night has passed, darkness succumbs to the overbearing gleam of the sun as <I>twilight</I> approaches.<BR><BR>So many things going on right now... But then when I really think about it, it's of nothing to compare with others. In hopes to decipher the thin red line between my goals and my obstacles, I bend time to benefit my needs. Thus, when you give alms, sound no trumpet before you, as the hypocrites do in the synagogues and in the streets, that they may be praised by men. </FONT></P> <P><FONT face=arial color=#333333 size=1><B>Truly, I say to you, they have received their reward. </FONT></P></B> <P><FONT face=arial color=#333333 size=1>But when you give alms, do not let your left hand know what your right hand is doing, so that your alms may be in secret; and your Father who sees in secret will reward you. </FONT></P> <P><FONT face=arial color=#333333 size=1>And when you pray, you must not be like the hypocrites; <I><B>for they love to stand and pray in the synagogues and at the street corners, that they may be seen by men. </I></FONT></P> <P><FONT face=arial color=#333333 size=1>Truly, I say to you, they have received their reward. </FONT></P> <P><FONT face=arial color=#333333 size=1>But when you pray, <B>go into your room and shut the door and pray to your Father who is in secret; <I>and your Father who sees in secret will reward you.</I></B> And in praying do not heap up empty phrases as the Gentiles do; for they think that they will be heard for their many words. Do not be like them, for your Father knows what you need before you ask him. </FONT></P> <P><FONT face=arial color=#333333 size=1>Pray then like this: Our Father who art in heaven, Hallowed be thy name. Thy kingdom come. Thy will be done, On earth as it is in heaven. Give us this day our daily bread; And forgive us our debts, As we also have forgiven our debtors; And lead us not into temptation, But deliver us from evil. For if you forgive men their trespasses, your heavenly Father also will forgive you; but if you do not forgive men their trespasses, neither will your Father forgive your trespasses. </FONT></P> <P><FONT face=arial color=#333333 size=1><B><I>And when you fast, do not look dismal, like the hypocrites, for they disfigure their faces that their fasting may be seen by men.</I><BR><BR>Truly, I say to you, they have received their reward.</B><BR><BR><I>But when you fast, anoint your head and wash your face, that your fasting may not be seen by men but by your Father who is in secret; and your Father who sees in secret will reward <B>you.</I></B></FONT> <B><I>Matthew 6:1-18</I></B><BR><BR></B></B><B>SO BASICALLY...</B> And this is all true. What this is saying is that <B>LENT</B> is <I>not</I> about feeling miserable. <B>LENT</B> is about realizing you have better things to do that sit in front of the computer all day.. Or lay on your bed while you could be out doing something productive. This is saying <B>BE YOU!</B> <B><I>WHO GIVES FOUR AND A HALF SHITS WHAT OTHER PEOPLE THINK OF YOU!!!</B></I> Tu es tres stupide, you halfwit, you.. All you who do it for the glory of being under the spotlight. Talking just for the sake of talking, not for the sake of something worth being said. Ok, yes we're all allowed to have fun... But there are always lines - thin thin lines - that can be drawn right where we can't see them. <B>The Gospel is saying..</B> i think.. That people shouldn't be worried about what goes around, around them too much. Because people do.. For example "o Lent.. i'm giving so much up and it's gonna be hell".. That's not the point of Lent is it?? It's the whole - being able to give something you use or see or whatever on an every day basis, and just being able to live without it - in happiness. <I>"Fuck the computer,</I> i told my brother Louie, <I>you live as if you needed it in your back pocket! Do you eat the computer for lunch?? Do you put it on before you go to school?? Do you need it to keep you warm at night?? Do you lay on top of it at night?? - <B>no</B>"</I> People, this is Lent. If you're not one to recognize Lent as a particular season - consider this blog as a wake up call, or to others a big slap in the face.
